 kya he digital karency?digital karency internet par chalane vaali ek virtual karency hai
 The virtual currency on the Internet started in January 2009 as Bitcoin
 is virtual karency kaa istemaal kar duniya ke kisi kone main kisi vyakti ko pement kiya ja saktaa he or sabase khaas baat yah he ki is bhugtan ke liye kisi bank ko madhyam banane kii bhi jarurat nahin padati
 How Digital Currency Works? The use of bitcoin is based on peer to peer technology
 iskaa matlab ki bitcoin kii madad se tranjaction do computer ke bich kiya ja saktaa he
 No Guardian or Central Bank is required for this transaction
 bitcoin open sorce karency he jahaan koi bhi isaki dizin se lekar control ko apane haath main rakh saktaa he
 Transactions can be done through this medium as no registration or ID is required
 is madhyam se tranjaction kii tamaam aisi khubia he jo maujuuda samay main koibanking tranjactionanheen detii
 Who started Bitcoin? Bitcoin was started in January 2009 by an unknown person
 is vyakti ne apana upnaam santoshi naakamoto bataaya or isse zyada apane bare main koi jaankaree nahin di
 However, this unknown person left the bitcoin project in 2010, after which bitcoin increased its business manifold
 maujuuda samay main bitcoin kii technology puri tarah se open sorce hone ke kaaran iske code main koi bhi parivartan kar saktaa he
 What is the important features of bitcoin? Bitcoin can easily transact between two people on the internet
 is tranjaction main shaamil donon logon ke bich jaan pahchaan hona jaruri nahin he
 Nor does it require government, bank or any agency to complete this transaction
 ek baar bitcoin ke madhyam se tranjaction ho jane ke baad ise cancel nahin kiya ja saktaa he
 This transaction can be executed in a few seconds and bitcoin is available to do other transactions immediately as soon as the transaction takes place
 global karency market main trade hota he bitcoinbitcoin kii 2009 main lonching ke baad lagaataar lokapriyata main ijapha hua he

terror attacks in the national capital, was granted bail by a special NIA court here today
 jila nyaayadhish aies mehta ne 20 hajaar rupee ke nijee muchalke tathaa itani hi raashi kii jamaanat dene par liyakat ko jamaanat par reeha karne ke aadesh die

 45varshiya liyakat ko unke parivaar ke saath 20 march ko uttar pradesh ke gorakhpur main bharat-nepal seemaa paar karte samay giraftaar kiya gaya tha
 Liaquat said that he had come to surrender under the rehabilitation policy of the Jammu and Kashmir government
 tippaniyan The Delhi Police, who arrested him soon after crossing the border, alleged that Liaquat was involved in a conspiracy to carry out terror attacks in the national capital before Holi

 jaidi ne kaha, ‘ham jald hi ek sarvadaleey baithak karenge jisamen unhen bataaya jayega ki hamaari iviem hamaari prashasnic evam takneekee suraksha pranali ke mutabik kis tarah se chhedchhad se mukt or surakshit hai
 ' haal hi main 16 vipakshi partiyon ne chunaav ayog se matdaan patr vyavastha kii ore lautne kaa anurodh karte hue daawa kiya tha ki iviem main logon kaa vishwaas khatm ho gaya he
 The Chief Election Commissioner also said that the Election Commission plans to organize a challenge in this regard, whose time is being considered
 samajha jaataa he ki chunaav ayog ek khuli chunauti dekar kisi se bhi yah kehane vaala he ki vah iviem ke durupyog ke andeh ko dur karne ke liye use hack karne kii koshish kar sakate hai
 The Election Commission also said that the Commission has ordered for the supply of VVPAT machines for use in elections

5 million vvpats to two psus - Bharat Electronics Limited (BEA) and Electronic Corporation of India (ECI)
 ’ unhone kaha ki ummid he ki sitambar, 2018 tak kareeb 15 lakh vivipieti mashine taiyaar ho jaaengi
 The commission aims to use the VVPAT in all upcoming elections

 police ne farji company ke shaatir maalik ko giraftaar kar liya he
 The accused owner used to get upset about his goods on the pretext of getting the goods transferred cheaply
 police ke mutabik, aaropee kaa naam lalit sharma he
 Lalit created an unofficial website of the packers and movers company
 yah company logon ke saamaan ko ek jagah se duusari jagah par saste main le jane kii sarvice detii thi
 Accused Lalit used to meet his victim in a very professional manner
 unka bharosa jeetne ke baad yah unka saamaan lekar gaayab ho jaataa tha
 This was revealed when Manoj Shrivastava, who was cheated by a fake company, filed a case against the accused Lalit
 privet form main karyrat manoj ne bataaya ki unhen apana saamaan dilli se lakhanu bhejnaa tha
 He was looking for the goods transfer company online
 jiske baad manoj ne farji pakars or movers ke maalik lalit se sampark kiya
 Lalit agreed to take Manoj's goods from Delhi to Lucknow at a very cheap price
 lalit ne manoj ko do dinon main saamaan lakhanu pahunchane kaa vaada kiya

 do din biit jane ke baad jab manoj kaa saamaan nahin pahunchaa to usne lalit ko phone kiya
 Lalit's phone got locked
 manoj ne turant is baat kii shikaayat police se kii
 Malviya Nagar Police arrested the accused Lalit from Bhiwani on Friday
 police ne manoj kaa gharelu saamaan bhi baraamad kar liya he
 Police is currently interrogating the accused and finding out about the other members of the gang
 patni ke liye pyaar jataane main kanjusee mat kijiye kyonki yah aapke daanpaty jivan kii safalataa kii kunjee sabit ho saktaa he
 In some countries, the name of the wife has been dedicated on 8 March
 aap bhi is din apni ardhangini ke samaksh prem kaa izhaar kijiye or iskaa karishma dekhiye
 Indian people are not very familiar with 'wife's Day', which is celebrated in Western countries
 lekin adhiktar kii raay he ki is din patniyon ko khush karne ke liye ‘main aapkaa hi hum’, ‘ai lav you’, ‘tumhaare sivaay main kisi or ke bare main sochataa bhi nahin saktaa’ jaise filmi shabd or vaakya kahen jaaen to daanpaty jivan sukhi ho saktaa he
 This day is very popular in countries like America and people there say their mind through greeting cards on this day to please wives
 manovaigyanikon kaa maananaa he ki daanpaty jivan ko madhur banaae rakhane ke liye prem ke bol kaa bahut mahatv he or ‘ai lav you’ jaise shabd na sirf ek-duusare ke prati aaksharn badhaate hai balki ek-duusare ke prati vafadari kii bhaavana bhi paidaa karte hai
 Renuka Singh, a former member of the 'army Wives Welfare Association' (AWA), says that on occasions like 'wife's Day' two words of love for a wife must be spoken
 renuka kaa kahana he ki vaise to patni se pyaar ke izhaar ke liye kisi vishesh din kii jarurat nahin he lekin phir bhi sambandhon ko tarotaaja banaae rakhane ke liye aise dinon ko apnaane main koi buraai bhi nahin he
 He says that the way love is expressed by giving rose flowers on Valentine's Day, in the same way, a husband can enjoy his wife with a beautiful gift on 'wife's Day'
 maharishi dayanand vishvavidhyalay se jude manovaigyanik espi singh maanate hai ki daanpaty jivan ko sukhmay banaae rakhane ke liye kuch na kuch jarur karte rahanaa chahie nahin to kai baar sambandh ubaau hone lagate hai
 He said that days like 'wife's Day' can work to bring innovation in the relationship

 Asin told, i am satisfied with whatever work i have done so far
 bollywood main ye mere praarambhik varsh hai or main adhik se adhik logon ke bich pahuchanna chaahati hum or sirf vyavsaayik filmein hi mujhe aisa karne main madad kar sakati hai
 " unhone kaha, rachanaatmak santushti mere liye bahut mahatvapurn he
 Right now i am looking for characters who are in commercial format and can give me creative satisfaction
 asin (26) ne varsh 2008 main ai film 'gazani' se bollywood main kadam rakhaa

 bollywood se pehle vah dakshin kii filmon main bhi acha naam kama chuki he

 tippaniyan His next film 'bol Bachchan' is releasing this Friday
 film kaa nirdesan rohit shetty ne kiya he
 Asin said that his character in the film is very practical and for that he did not even have to do homework
 film main sania kii bhoomika mere liye bahut adhik chunauteepurn nahin thi
 i didn't have to do too much homework and research
 asin ne bataaya, abhi tak maine jo bhi kaam kiya he, main usase santusht hum
 These are my early years in Bollywood and i want to reach more and more people and only commercial films can help me do that

 pali or sanskrit kaa sinhalai bhashaa par kaaphi prabhaav he
